\item[{output files will be created\char`\"{}\char`\"{}within that}]{directory, }
\item[{with file-\/names based on the test\char`\"{}\char`\"{}executable's name}]{and, }
\item[{if}]{necessary, }
\item[{made unique by adding\char`\"{}\char`\"{}digits.\char`\"{}}]{}
